A_DT direct_JJ consequence_NN of_IN this_DT fact_NN is_VBZ :_: The_DT electrostatic_JJ work_NN done_VBN on_IN a_DT charged_JJ particle_NN as_IN it_PRP moves_VBZ from_IN one_CD point_NN to_TO another_DT is_VBZ independent_JJ of_IN the_DT path_NN taken_VBN by_IN the_DT particle_NN and_CC depends_VBZ on_IN only_RB the_DT positions_NNS of_IN the_DT endpoints_NNS of_IN the_DT path_NN ._.

Imagine_VB ,_, for_IN example_NN ,_, lifting_VBG a_DT particle_NN from_IN A_NN to_TO B_NN along_IN curved_JJ path_NN 2_CD in_IN Figure_NNP 25.6_CD a_DT instead_RB of_IN along_RB straight_JJ path_NN 1_CD ._.

In_IN other_JJ words_NNS ,_, the_DT electrostatic_JJ work_NN on_IN the_DT particle_NN along_IN path_NN 2_CD -LRB-_-LRB- or_CC any_DT other_JJ path_NN from_IN <var>_NN to_TO <var>_NN -RRB-_-RRB- is_VBZ equal_JJ to_TO that_DT along_IN path_NN 1_CD ._.
Figure_NN 25.6_CD c_NN shows_VBZ how_WRB this_DT argument_NN can_MD be_VB generalized_VBN to_TO a_DT nonuniform_JJ electric_JJ field_NN ._.
Imagine_VB a_DT particle_NN being_VBG moved_VBN from_IN point_NN <var>_NN to_TO point_NN <var>_NN along_IN the_DT gray_JJ trajectory_NN in_IN the_DT electric_JJ field_NN caused_VBN by_IN an_DT object_NN carrying_VBG a_DT charge_NN at_IN the_DT origin_NN ._.

The_DT electrostatic_JJ work_NN done_VBN on_IN the_DT particle_NN along_IN any_DT path_NN from_IN <var>_NN to_TO <var>_NN is_VBZ thus_RB the_DT same_JJ as_IN the_DT electrostatic_JJ work_NN done_VBN from_IN <var>_NN to_TO <var>_NN ._.
Checkpoint_NN 25.4_CD shows_VBZ that_IN the_DT electrostatic_JJ work_NN done_VBN on_IN a_DT charged_JJ particle_NN that_IN moves_NNS around_IN a_DT closed_JJ path_NN any_DT closed_JJ path_NN in_IN an_DT electrostatic_JJ field_NN is_VBZ zero_NN ._.
We_PRP obtained_VBD a_DT similar_JJ result_NN for_IN the_DT work_NN done_VBN by_IN the_DT gravitational_JJ force_NN -LRB-_-LRB- Eq_NN ._. 13.17_CD -RRB-_-RRB- ._.
The_DT physical_JJ reason_NN for_IN this_DT result_NN is_VBZ that_IN the_DT electric_JJ force_NN between_IN two_CD charged_JJ particles_NNS ,_, like_IN the_DT gravitational_JJ force_NN between_IN two_CD objects_NNS that_WDT have_VBP mass_NN ,_, is_VBZ nondissipative_JJ :_: When_WRB charged_VBN particles_NNS are_VBP moved_VBN around_RB in_IN electrostatic_JJ fields_NNS ,_, no_DT energy_NN is_VBZ irreversibly_RB converted_VBN to_TO other_JJ forms_NNS of_IN energy_NN ._.
This_DT is_VBZ so_RB because_IN the_DT electric_JJ interaction_NN is_VBZ nondissipative_JJ ._.
The_DT third_JJ part_NN of_IN Checkpoint_NN 25.5_CD demonstrates_VBZ a_DT very_RB important_JJ point_NN :_: The_DT electrostatic_JJ work_NN done_VBN on_IN a_DT charged_JJ particle_NN is_VBZ proportional_JJ to_TO the_DT charge_NN carried_VBN by_IN that_DT particle_NN ._.
This_DT means_VBZ that_IN once_RB we_PRP have_VBP calculated_VBN the_DT electrostatic_JJ work_NN done_VBN on_IN a_DT particle_NN carrying_VBG a_DT charge_NN q_NN along_IN some_DT path_NN in_IN an_DT electrostatic_JJ field_NN ,_, we_PRP do_VBP n't_RB need_VB to_TO carry_VB out_RP the_DT whole_JJ calculation_NN again_RB if_IN we_PRP are_VBP interested_JJ in_IN the_DT electrostatic_JJ work_NN done_VBN on_IN another_DT particle_NN carrying_VBG a_DT charge_NN 2q_NN ._.
We_PRP know_VBP that_IN the_DT electrostatic_JJ work_NN done_VBN on_IN the_DT second_JJ particle_NN is_VBZ twice_RB the_DT electrostatic_JJ work_NN done_VBN on_IN the_DT first_JJ ._.
Thus_RB ,_, if_IN we_PRP know_VBP the_DT electrostatic_JJ work_NN done_VBN on_IN a_DT particle_NN carrying_VBG a_DT unit_NN positive_JJ charge_NN along_IN some_DT path_NN ,_, then_RB we_PRP know_VBP the_DT electrostatic_JJ work_NN done_VBN on_IN a_DT particle_NN carrying_VBG any_DT charge_NN between_IN the_DT same_JJ two_CD points_NNS !_.
We_PRP therefore_RB introduce_VBP a_DT new_JJ quantity_NN ,_, called_VBN electrostatic_JJ potential_JJ difference_NN -LRB-_-LRB- or_CC simply_RB potential_JJ difference_NN -RRB-_-RRB- ,_, defined_VBN as_IN :_:
The_DT potential_JJ difference_NN between_IN point_NN <var>_NN and_CC point_NN <var>_NN in_IN an_DT electrostatic_JJ field_NN is_VBZ equal_JJ to_TO the_DT negative_NN of_IN the_DT electrostatic_JJ work_NN per_IN unit_NN charge_NN done_VBN on_IN a_DT charged_JJ particle_NN as_IN it_PRP moves_VBZ from_IN <var>_NN to_TO <var>_NN ._.

Figure_NN 26.15_CD shows_VBZ what_WP happens_VBZ when_WRB a_DT dielectricfilled_JJ capacitor_NN is_VBZ connected_VBN to_TO a_DT battery_NN ._.

As_IN shown_VBN in_IN Figure_NNP 26.15_CD b_NN ,_, the_DT polarization_NN of_IN the_DT dielectric_NN causes_VBZ a_DT negative_JJ bound_VBN surface_NN charge_NN next_JJ to_TO the_DT positive_JJ capacitor_NN plate_NN ;_: the_DT sum_NN of_IN the_DT free_JJ charge_NN on_IN the_DT conductor_NN and_CC the_DT adjoining_JJ bound_VBN surface_NN charge_NN must_MD still_RB be_VB equal_JJ to_TO +_CC <var>_NN ._.

-LRB-_-LRB- Nonparaxial_JJ rays_NNS are_VBP shifted_VBN significantly_RB ;_: our_PRP$ treatment_NN of_IN lenses_NNS in_IN this_DT chapter_NN is_VBZ restricted_JJ to_TO images_NNS formed_VBN by_IN paraxial_JJ rays_NNS ._. -RRB-_-RRB-
